## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> SHIPMENT_CREATED
    SHIPMENT_CREATED --> ASSET_ASSIGNED
    ASSET_ASSIGNED --> PICKED_UP
    PICKED_UP --> DEPARTED_PICK_UP
    DEPARTED_PICK_UP --> ARRIVED
    ARRIVED --> ARRIVED_AT_DROP_OFF
    ARRIVED_AT_DROP_OFF --> DEPARTED_DROP_OFF
    DEPARTED_DROP_OFF --> DELIVERED
    DELIVERED --> [*]
    
    SHIPMENT_CREATED --> SHIPMENT_UPDATED
    SHIPMENT_UPDATED --> SHIPMENT_CANCELLED
    SHIPMENT_CANCELLED --> [*]
    
    ASSET_ASSIGNED --> ASSET_UNASSIGNED
    ASSET_UNASSIGNED --> ASSET_ASSIGNED
    
    DEPARTED_PICK_UP --> BEHIND_SCHEDULE
    BEHIND_SCHEDULE --> BEHIND_SCHEDULE_CLEARED
    BEHIND_SCHEDULE_CLEARED --> DEPARTED_PICK_UP
    
    DEPARTED_PICK_UP --> OFF_ROUTE
    OFF_ROUTE --> CLEAR_OFF_ROUTE
    CLEAR_OFF_ROUTE --> DEPARTED_PICK_UP
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Shipment Created] --> B{Mode Type?}
    B -->|Truck/LTL| C[Asset Assigned]
    B -->|Rail| D[Rail Picked Up]
    B -->|Intermodal| E[Multiple Legs]
    
    C --> F[Picked Up]
    F --> G[Departed Origin]
    G --> H[In Transit]
    
    D --> I[Rail Departed]
    I --> J[Rail Arrived]
    J --> K[Rail Delivered]
    
    E --> L[First Leg Complete]
    L --> M[Second Leg Start]
    M --> N[Final Destination]
    
    H --> O{Status Check}
    O -->|On Time| P[Arrived at Destination]
    O -->|Delayed| Q[Behind Schedule]
    O -->|Issue| R[Exception Raised]
    
    Q --> S[Cleared]
    S --> P
    
    R --> T{Exception Type}
    T -->|Backorder| U[Backorder]
    T -->|Off Route| V[Off Route]
    T -->|No Activity| W[No Activity]
    T -->|Carrier Delay| X[Carrier Delayed]
    
    U --> Y[Cleared]
    V --> Y
    W --> Y
    X --> Y
    Y --> P
    
    P --> Z[Delivered]
    K --> Z
    N --> Z
```
